# Security Audit: Missing Authentication Middleware in HTTP Handlers

## Your Task

Your security team is conducting an audit of the Grafana observability stack.
The pattern in `grafana/grafana` (local) shows proper authentication middleware
usage: HTTP handlers are wrapped with `middleware.AuthenticateUser` to enforce
tenant authentication.

Your task is to **find Go source files in the MCP-only repositories** (Loki
and/or Mimir) that register HTTP handlers or routes **without applying
authentication middleware** such as `middleware.AuthenticateUser`.

For each file found, report:
- The repository (e.g., `sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki`)
- The file path within the repository
- The specific endpoint path(s) registered without authentication

## Context

You are auditing a microservices observability stack. The local `grafana/grafana`
repo correctly wraps its compactor deletion endpoint with authentication:

```go
// Example from pkg/compactor/ui.go — middleware applied correctly
mw := middleware.Merge(
    middleware.AuthenticateUser,
    deletion.TenantMiddleware(c.limits),
)
```

In contrast, some files in the MCP-only repos may register endpoints directly
with `mux.HandleFunc(...)` without any auth middleware wrapping, or use
`RegisterRoute(...)` with `auth=false`. These are the files your audit needs
to surface.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains all repositories:
- `grafana/grafana` at v11.4.0 → `/workspace/grafana`
- `grafana/loki` at v3.3.4 → `/workspace/loki`

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {
      "repo": "sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki",
      "path": "relative/path/to/file.go",
      "endpoints": ["/endpoint/path/1", "/endpoint/path/2"]
    }
  ],
  "text": "Narrative citing specific repos, file paths, and endpoint paths registered without authentication."
}
```

**Important**: Use exact repo identifiers as they appear in Sourcegraph. The MCP-only repos to audit are `sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki` and `sg-benchmarks/grafana-mimir`. Note: the local `/workspace/loki` directory maps to `sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki` in Sourcegraph — use `sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki` as the `repo` value in your answer. The oracle checks for `pkg/dataobj/explorer/service.go` in `sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki`.
**Note**: Sourcegraph MCP tools return repo names with a `github.com/` prefix (e.g., `github.com/sg-benchmarks/kubernetes-client-go`). Strip this prefix in your answer — use `sg-benchmarks/kubernetes-client-go`, NOT `github.com/sg-benchmarks/kubernetes-client-go`.

Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find the Go files that register handlers without authentication middleware?
- **Provenance**: Does your answer cite the specific repos and file paths?

    25→func (d *Distributor) OTLPPushHandler(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    26→	interceptor := newOtelErrorHeaderInterceptor(w)
    27→	d.pushHandler(interceptor, r, push.ParseOTLPRequest)
    28→}
    29→
    30→// otelErrorHeaderInterceptor maps 500 errors to 503.
    31→// According to the OTLP specification, 500 errors are never retried on the client side, but 503 are.
    32→type otelErrorHeaderInterceptor struct {
    33→	http.ResponseWriter
    34→}
    35→
    36→func newOtelErrorHeaderInterceptor(w http.ResponseWriter) *otelErrorHeaderInterceptor {
    37→	return &otelErrorHeaderInterceptor{ResponseWriter: w}
    38→}
    39→
    40→func (i *otelErrorHeaderInterceptor) WriteHeader(statusCode int) {
    41→	if statusCode == http.StatusInternalServerError {
    42→		statusCode = http.StatusServiceUnavailable
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	i.ResponseWriter.WriteHeader(statusCode)
    46→}
    47→

    49→	logger := util_log.WithContext(r.C

    15→func CorsMiddleware() mux.MiddlewareFunc {
    16→	return func(h http.Handler) http.Handler {
    17→		return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    18→			w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
    19→			w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Headers", "Content-Type")
    20→			if r.Method == http.MethodOptions {
    21→				w.WriteHeader(200)
    22→				return
    23→			}
    24→			h.ServeHTTP(w, r)
    25→		})
    26→	}
    27→}
    28→
    29→type LogQLAnalyzeHandler struct {
    30→	analyzer logQLAnalyzer
    31→}
    32→
    33→func (s *LogQLAnalyzeHandler) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
    34→	payload, err := io.ReadAll(req.Body)
    35→	if err != nil {
    36→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable to read request body")
    37→		return
    38→	}
    39→	requestBody := &Request{}
    40→	err = json.Unmarshal(payload, requestBody)
    41→	if err != nil {
    42→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable unmarshal request body")
    43→		return
    44→	}
    45→	result, err := s.analyzer.analyze(requestBody.Query, requestBody.Logs)
    46→	if err != nil {
    47→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable to analyze query")
    48→		return
    49→	}
    50→	responseBody, err := json.Marshal(result)
    51→	if err != nil {
    52→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusInternalServerError, "can not marshal the response")
    53→		retu
... (truncated)

     1→package deletion

     8→
     9→func TenantMiddleware(limits Limits, next http.Handler) http.Handler {
    10→	return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    11→		ctx := r.Context()
    12→		userID, err := tenant.TenantID(ctx)
    13→		if err != nil {
    14→			http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
    15→			return
    16→		}
    17→
    18→		hasDelete, err := validDeletionLimit(limits, userID)
    19→		if err != nil {
    20→			http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
    21→			return
    22→		}
    23→
    24→		if !hasDelete {
    25→			http.Error(w, deletionNotAvailableMsg, http.StatusForbidden)
    26→			return
    27→		}
    28→
    29→		next.ServeHTTP(w, r)
    30→	})
    31→}

    15→func CorsMiddleware() mux.MiddlewareFunc {
    16→	return func(h http.Handler) http.Handler {
    17→		return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    18→			w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
    19→			w.Header().Set("Access-Control-Allow-Headers", "Content-Type")
    20→			if r.Method == http.MethodOptions {
    21→				w.WriteHeader(200)
    22→				return
    23→			}
    24→			h.ServeHTTP(w, r)
    25→		})
    26→	}
    27→}

    36→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable to read request body")
    37→		return
    38→	}
    39→	requestBody := &Request{}
    40→	err = json.Unmarshal(payload, requestBody)
    41→	if err != nil {
    42→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable unmarshal request body")
    43→		return
    44→	}
    45→	result, err := s.analyzer.analyze(requestBody.Query, requestBody.Logs)
    46→	if err != nil {
    47→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusBadRequest, "unable to analyze query")
    48→		return
    49→	}
    50→	responseBody, err := json.Marshal(result)
    51→	if err != nil {
    52→		writeError(req.Context(), w, err, http.StatusInternalServerError, "can not marshal the response")

     9→func TenantMiddleware(limits Limits, next http.Handler) http.Handler {

    11→		ctx := r.Context()

    14→			http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)

    16→		}
    17→

    19→		if err != nil {
    20→			http.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
    21→			return
    22→		}
    23→

    25→			http.Error(w, deletionNotAvailableMsg, http.StatusForbidden)

    27→		}

## Security Audit Results

I've identified HTTP handlers without authentication middleware in both Loki and Mimir repositories and created a comprehensive report at `/workspace/answer.json`.

### Key Findings:

**sg-benchmarks/grafana-loki (2 files):**
1. **cmd/logql-analyzer/main.go** - 5 unprotected endpoints including `/api/logql-analyze`, sizing endpoints, and `/ready`
2. **pkg/loki/modules.go** - 9 ring/cluster management endpoints (e.g., `/ring`, `/distributor/ring`, `/memberlist`, `/compactor/ring`) registered without `HTTPAuthMiddleware` wrapping

**sg-benchmarks/grafana-mimir (1 file):**
1. **pkg/api/api.go** - 34+ endpoints registered with `auth=false` parameter, including:
   - Ring endpoints (distributor, ingester, ruler, store-gateway, compactor)
   - Operational endpoints (flush, shutdown, prepare-downscale)
   - Status and configuration endpoints
   - Cluster membership endpoints

### Pattern Identified:
- In **Loki**: Handlers registered on `t.Server.HTTP` without `.Wrap()` middleware, unlike properly protected endpoints that use `httpMiddleware.Wrap()` 
- In **Mimir**: Handlers registered via `RegisterRoute()` with third parameter set to `false` instead of `true`

The answer file contains the complete inventory with file paths, endpoint paths, and a detailed risk assessment explaining how these unprotected endpoints expose sensitive operational and cluster topology information.
